为持续保障民航安全运行，确保疫情防控期间国际航空货运供应链稳定。现向所有在我国境 内执行任务的外国航空公司，特别是疫情防控期间临时执行加班任务的外航机组，发布安全提示 : 1.提醒飞行员 （ 1）应严格按照管制员指令运行，如对指令存有疑问，则一定要向管制员证实清楚指令。 （ 2）提醒监听复诵管制指令，特别是关于航路、高度、频率、进离场航线和地面滑行方面的指令予以重点关注，避免发生错误。特别提醒机组首都机场进  离场程序、地面滑行路线较复杂予以特别关注。（ 3）在中国境内飞行的高度层使用公制计量，进出中国境内，注意高度层转换。RVSM空域按照中国 AIP规定的方式执行。 （ 4）在中国境内执行飞行任务时，应遵守全程收听 121.5应急频率的规定，避免机组失去通信联系。 2.提醒各航空公司 通过商业航班运输防疫物资中的危险品，如呼吸机中的锂电池、酒精类洗手液等，需符合 ICAO《危险 物品安全航空运输技术细则》（ DOC 9284）的有关要求。	1

.航空器安全状况通报的时间,范围和报告要求 （一）时间2023年 3月 3日 0时至2023年 3月 14日 23 时 59分 . （二）临时空中限制区范围以天安门为中心半径 150公里划设临时空中限制区 . （三）报告要求 1.以天安门为中心半径 200公里划设安全状态报告圈 .凡去往北京首都机场，北京大兴机场及天津滨海机场落地的航空器，在进入安全状态报告圈前主动向相关管制部门报告航班号（呼号），位置及航空器安全状况.安保报告不正常，或证实安保状态时不予回复的航空器，不得进入 150公里临时空中限制区 . 2.石家庄正定机场，乌兰察布集宁机场，大同云冈机场，张家口宁远机场，承德普宁机场，唐山三女河机场，秦皇岛北戴河机场起飞去往北京首都机场，北京大兴机场及天津滨海机场落地的航空器，当地管制部门须执行起飞前证实安全状况 .即航空器首次联系管制部门时，须由相关管制部门证实航空器安保状况为正常后，方可由发布相关管制放行许可后起飞 . 二 .明确各航路航线飞行时位置报告点 1.沿 W157经 TUMLO 16.偏离上述航线的航空器在切过上述报告点前报告安全状况 . 17.未在上述范围内航线飞行，需进入临时空中限制区且飞往北京首都机场，北京大兴机场，天津滨海机场落地的航空器，在进入安全状态报告圈前报告安全状况 . 三 .管制部门之间的协调 1.向北京区域管制中心报告的航空器，由北京区域管制中心按照操作指引和相关要求进行处置 . 2.向石家庄正定塔台管制室，乌兰察布集宁机场塔台管制室，大同云冈机场塔台管制室，张家口宁远机场塔台管制室，承德普宁机场塔台管制  室，唐山三女河机场塔台管制室 及秦皇岛北戴河机场塔台管制室报告安保状态的航空器，由相关管制单位按照报告要求进行处置 .安全状态报告不正常的航空器，由负责管制的单位指挥航空器原地等待暂缓移交，并立即向北京区域管制中心进行通报，并根据北京区域管制中心反馈的处置要求执行 . 3.安保报告正常的，管制部门间无需进行通报.安保报告不正常的，管制部门在移交前必须进行特殊通报. 四 .安保报告标准通话用语 P：北  京， XXX101， ...，安保正常 . BEIJING， SECURITY NORMAL,XXX101. 如机组未主动通报安保状况，管制员应主动询问C： XXX101，北京，确认安保状况 . MILITARY EXERCISE AIR DEFENDER 2023 (12 - 22 JUN 2023). 德国军演摘要 1、德国对于空中卫士2023”军事演习，将建立临时禁区和危险区（NfL 2023-1-2767）以及额外的飞行计划缓冲区。演习分为三种场景（东部、南部和北部），每天连续飞行（周六和周日除外） 2、3.限制和危险区域 3.1所有已建立的限制区域（ED-R）的飞行限制类型 在以下地区，禁止未参加空中卫士2023”演习的飞机飞行。飞行限制不适用于国家飞机、警察部队的航班、执行救援和灾害控制任务的航班、救护车航班和经空中交通管制主管部门事先许可的红十字与红新月联会航班。可以通过无线电话提出穿越该地区的请求。 3.2所有已确定危险区域的航空危险类型（ED-D） 由于空中卫士2023”演习有关的军事训练飞行，所有未参加演习的飞行员都被紧急要求避开危险区域。 经系统检查，受影响的公司航路具体情况如下，请导航室具体评估： （1）EAST东部临时区域 活动时间：2023年6月12日至16日，19日至22日，每天0800-1200 当前有效公司航路 ----------------------ED10065 KILNU - ZNY DE..AIRSPACE WILMINGTON,  DELAWARE..TEMPORARY FLIGHT RESTRICTIONS.        FEBRUARY 24-27, 2023 LOCAL.  PURSUANT TO 49 USC 40103(B)(3), THE FEDERAL AVIATION ADMINISTRATION (FAA) CLASSIFIES THE AIRSPACE DEFINED IN THIS NOTAM AS 'NTL DEFENSE AIRSPACE'. PILOTS WHO DO NOT ADHERE TO THE FOLLOWING PROC MAY BE INTERCEPTED, DETAINED AND INTERVIEWED BY LAW ENFORCEMENT/SECURITY PERSONNEL. ANY OF THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL ACTIONS MAY ALSO BE TAKEN AGAINST A PILOT WHO DOES NOT COMPLY WITH THE RQMNTS OR  ANY SPECIAL INSTRUCTIONS OR PROC ANNOUNCED IN THIS NOTAM: A) THE FAA MAY TAKE ADMINISTRATIVE ACTION, INCLUDING IMPOSING CIVIL PENALTIES AND THE SUSPENSION OR REVOCATION OF AIRMEN CERTIFICATES? OR  B) THE UNITED STATES GOVERNMENT MAY PURSUE CRIMINAL CHARGES, INCLUDING CHARGES UNDER 49 USC SECTION 46307? OR  C) THE UNITED STATES GOVERNMENT MAY USE DEADLY FORCE AGAINST THE AIRBORNE ACFT, IF IT IS DETERMINED THAT THE ACFT POSES AN IMMINENT SECURITY THREAT.   PURSUANT TO 14 CFR 91.141, ALL ACFT FLT OPS INCLUDING REMOTE CONTROLLED ACFT OPS ARE PROHIBITED: WI AN AREA DEFINED AS 28NM   ZNY DE..AIRSPACE WILMINGTON,  DELAWARE..TEMPORARY FLIGHT RADIUS OF 394400N0753953W (DQO331004.3) SFC-17999FT MSL?  EXCLUDING AN AREA DEFINED AS 1.5NM RADIUS OF 393400N0761234W (DQO267028.7) SFC-17999FT MSL?  EXCLUDING AN AREA DEFINED AS 2.5NM RADIUS OF 392756N0761006W (BAL063029.0) SFC-17999FT MSL? WI AN AREA DEFINED AS 12NM RADIUS OF 394400N0753953W (DQO331004.3) SFC-17999FT MSL EFFECTIVE 2302242230 UTC (1730 LOCAL 02/24/23) UNTIL 2302271600 UTC (1100 LOCAL 02/27/23). EXCEPT AS SPECIFIED BELOW AND/OR UNLESS AUTHORIZED BY ATC IN CONSULTATION WITH THE AIR TRAFFIC SECURITY COORDINATOR VIA THE DOMESTIC EVENTS NETWORK (DEN):   ZNY DE..AIRSPACE WILMINGTON, DELAWARE..TEMPORARY FLIGHT A. ALL AIRCRAFT OPERATIONS WITHIN THE 12 NMR AREA(S) LISTED ABOVE, KNOWN AS THE INNER CORE(S),    ARE PROHIBITED EXCEPT FOR: APPROVED LAW ENFORCEMENT, MILITARY AIRCRAFT DIRECTLY SUPPORTING    THE UNITED STATES SECRET SERVICE (USSS) AND THE OFFICE OF THE PRESIDENT OF THE UNITED STATES,    APPROVED AIR AMBULANCE FLIGHTS, AND REGULARLY SCHEDULED COMMERCIAL PASSENGER AND ALL-CARGO    CARRIERS OPERATING UNDER ONE OF THE FOLLOWING TSA-APPROVED STANDARD SECURITY PROGRAMS/PROCEDURES    AND ARE ARRIVING INTO AND/OR DEPARTING FROM 14 CFR PART 139 AIRPORTS: AIRCRAFT OPERATOR STANDARD    SECURITY PROGRAM (AOSSP), FULL ALL-CARGO AIRCRAFT OPERATOR STANDARD SECURITY PROGRAM (FACAOSSP),    MODEL SECURITY PROGRAM (MSP), TWELVE FIVE STANDARD SECURITY PROGRAM ALL CARGO (TFSSP-ALL CARGO), OR  ALL-CARGO INTERNATIONAL SECURITY PROCEDURE(ACISP). ALL EMERGENCY/LIFE SAVING FLIGHT    (MEDICAL/LAW ENFORCEMENT/FIREFIGHTING) OPERATIONS  MUST COORDINATE WITH ATC PRIOR TO THEIR DEPARTURE    AT 215-492-4123/4185 TO AVOID POTENTIAL DELAYS. B. FOR OPERATIONS WITHIN THE AIRSPACE BETWEEN THE 12 NMR AND 28 NMR AREA(S) LISTED ABOVE, KNOWN AS    THE OUTER RING(S): ALL AIRCRAFT OPERATING WITHIN THE OUTER RING(S) LISTED ABOVE ARE LIMITED TO    AIRCRAFT ARRIVING OR DEPARTING LOCAL AIRFIELDS, AND WORKLOAD PERMITTING, ATC MAY AUTHORIZE TRANSIT    OPERATIONS. AIRCRAFT MAY NOT LOITER. ALL AIRCRAFT MUST BE ON AN ACTIVE IFR OR FILED VFR FLIGHT PLAN    WITH A DISCRETE CODE ASSIGNED BY AN AIR TRAFFIC CONTROL (ATC) FACILITY. AIRCRAFT MUST BE SQUAWKING    THE DISCRETE CODE PRIOR TO DEPARTURE AND AT ALL TIMES WHILE IN THE TFR AND MUST REMAIN IN TWO-WAY    RADIO COMMUNICATIONS WITH ATC. C. ALL FLIGHT OPERATIONS NOT COVERED IN PARAGRAPH A. WITHIN THE 12 NMR AREA MUST BE SECURITYSCREENED BY  TSA AT A GATEWAY AIRPORT PRIOR TO ARRIVING OR DEPARTING NEW CASTLE AIRPORT (KILG) .    AIRCRAFT OPERATORS MUST REGISTER WITH THE TSA FOR GATEWAY SCREENING NO LESS THAN 24 HOURS PRIOR TO    THEIR SCHEDULED DEPARTURE TIME. RESERVATIONS FOR SCREENING MAY BEGIN ON 02/23/2023 AND LAST THROUGH    THE DURATION OF THE EVENT BY CALLING TSA AT 610-537-9027. D. GATEWAY AIRPORTS HAVE BEEN CREATED AT NEW CASTLE AIRPORT (KILG) , ALLENTOWN INTERNATIONAL    AIRPORT (KABE) AND DULLES INTERNATIONAL AIRPORT（KIAD) BY TSA TO ACCOMMODATE AIRCRAFT ARRIVING OR    DEPARTING NEW CASTLE AIRPORT (KILG). E. TSA SCREENING WILL NOT BE AVAILABLE ON FRIDAY, 02/24/2023. TSA SCREENING WILL BE AVAILABLE    EFFECTIVE 2302251300 UTC (0800 LOCAL 02/25/23) TO 2302252200 UTC (1700 LOCAL 02/25/23). TSA    SCREENING WILL BE AVAILABLE 2302261300 UTC (0800 LOCAL 02/26/23) TO 2302262200 UTC (1700 LOCAL    02/26/23). TSA SCREENING WILL NOT BE AVAILABLE ON MONDAY, 02/27/2023. PILOTS, CREW AND PASSENGERS    MUST PROVIDE VALID GOVERNMENT-ISSUED PHOTO IDENTIFICATION TO THE TSA AT THE GATEWAY AIRPORT.    GATEWAY SCREENING WILL INCLUDE ID VERIFICATION AND VETTING OF ALL PILOTS, CREW AND PASSENGERS,    SCREENING OF PERSONS AND BAGGAGE, AND INSPECTION OF THE AIRCRAFT. NO FIREARMS ON BOARD AIRCRAFT WILL BE AUTHORIZED. NO GIFT WRAPPED PACKAGES. F. ON DEPARTURE FROM A GATEWAY AIRPORT AIRCRAFT MUST MAINTAIN RADIO CONTACT WITH ATC AND    CONTINUOUSLY SQUAWK AN ATC-ASSIGNED DISCRETE CODE. INTERMEDIATE STOPS WHILE ENROUTE ARE NOT AUTHORIZED UNLESS AN EMERGENCY EXISTS. G. THE FOLLOWING OPERATIONS ARE NOT AUTHORIZED WITHIN THIS TFR: FLIGHT TRAINING, PRACTICE    INSTRUMENT APPROACHES, AEROBATIC FLIGHT, GLIDER OPERATIONS, PARACHUTE OPERATIONS, ULTRALIGHT, HANG    GLIDING, BALLOON OPERATIONS, AGRICULTURE/CROP DUSTING, ANIMAL POPULATION CONTROL FLIGHT    OPERATIONS, BANNER TOWING OPERATIONS, SIGHTSEEING OPERATIONS, MAINTENANCE TEST FLIGHTS, MODEL AIRCRAFT OPERATIONS, MODEL ROCKETRY, UNMANNED    AIRCRAFT SYSTEMS (UAS), AND UTILITY AND PIPELINE    SURVEY OPERATIONS. H. UAS OPERATORS WHO DO NOT COMPLY WITH APPLICABLE AIRSPACE RESTRICTIONS ARE WARNED THAT PURSUANT TO    10 U.S.C. SECTION 130I AND 6 U.S.C. SECTION 124N,    THE DEPARTMENT OF DEFENSE (DOD) , THE DEPARTMENT OF HOMELAND SECURITY (DHS) OR THE DEPARTMENT OF    JUSTICE (DOJ) MAY TAKE SECURITY ACTION THAT   RESULTS IN THE INTERFERENCE, DISRUPTION, SEIZURE,    DAMAGING, OR DESTRUCTION OF UNMANNED AIRCRAFT DEEMED TO POSE A CREDIBLE SAFETY OR SECURITY    THREAT TO PROTECTED PERSONNEL, FACILITIES, OR ASSETS. I. THE SYSTEM OPERATIONS SUPPORT CENTER (SOSC), IS THE COORDINATION FACILITY FOR GOVERNMENT AGENCIES    AND IS AVAILABLE DAILY FROM 0700-2300 EASTERN,PHONE 202-267-8276 FOR COORDINATION. J. (THIS NOTAM IS ONLY FOR CHINA SOUTHERN AIRLINES) 结合一发失效复飞分析结果，A319-115 机型执行ZWTK航线时应遵循以下限制： 1.在签派放行时，15号跑道需要提高着陆标准运行，DA（H）需提高到12420’（1770’），VIS需提高到8000M，即按复飞梯度2.5%的运行标准掌握；33号跑道无特殊要求； 2.在飞行中，机组在执行15 号跑道进近程序时，其复飞决断高需调整为 1770FT，并爬升到13000FT 改平加速收襟翼。 According to Analysis of OEI GA, operation of A319-115 in ZWTK should follow the instructions below, 1.During dispatching flight, the operation standard of RWY15 should be raised so that the DA(H) should be raised to 12420’(1770’) and the VIS to 8000M which means to meet the operation standard of 2.5% GA GRAD.. There is no change to the standard of RWY33. 2.When the flight crew is approaching via RWY15, the DH should be raised to 1770’. Climb to 13000’ to level off and accelerate to retract the flaps when go around.	4

为持续保障民航安全运行，确保疫情防控期间国际航空货运供应链稳定。现向所有在我国境 内执行任务的外国航空公司，特别是疫情防控期间临时执行加班任务的外航机组，发布安全提示 : 1.提醒飞行员 （ 1）应严格按照管制员指令运行，如对指令存有疑问，则一定要向管制员证实清楚指令。 （ 2）提醒监听复诵管制指令，特别是关于航路、高度、频率、进离场航线和地面滑行方面的指令予以重点关注，避免发生错误。特别提醒机组首都机场进离场程序、地面滑行路线较复杂予以特别关注。 （ 3）在中国境内飞行的高度层使用公制计量，进出中国境内，注意高度层转换。 RVSM空域按照中国 AIP规定的方式执行。 （ 4）在中国境内执行飞行任务时，应遵守全程收听 121.5应急频率的规定，避免机组失去通信联系。 2.提醒各航空公司 通过商业航班运输防疫物资中的危险品，如呼吸机中的锂电池、酒精类洗手液等，需 符合 ICAO《危险物品安全航空运输技术细则》（ DOC9284）的有关要求。	4
